PORTMSE|TABLE|Table representing a service event. A service event is a web service request that executes either 1) as a result of a consumed Business Event message or 2) whenever a bulk feed is sent.
PORTMSM|TABLE|Table representing a SQL Definition for mapping SQL data to a service provider's API specification. This object defines a SQL statement that maps to a Data Mapping Record.

extracted from the database, evaluated and executed in SARRATE, the Admissions Rating Process.
SARRRFT|TABLE|This table contains Rating Factor Rules and Rating Factor Value definitions. The available values for specifying rules include term, level, campus, college, program, admit type, student type, residency and major.  Institutions
 can enter any combination of values to tailor the rating factors to meet their needs.  The value of a Rating Factor can be a static value or can be a key value that will be used in the generation of dynamic SQL to retrieve a factor value from the databas
e.

SVROAFA|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS application form tracking by applicant table is to track the application forms completed by the applicant via the OCAS web application.
SVROAFP|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS application form - program schedule maintenance table will be used to store the configuration of the application forms,
the programs offered in those application forms in a given term, start-date, semester and campus.
These program combinations are the ones that will be presented to the applicant when applying for Admissions via the web application.
 However, note that the applicant will be able to choose ONLY a maximum number of those programs depending on the max number
 that was configured for the application form in question (SVROAFR_MAX_NUM_CHOICES) in a given OCAS year.
SVROAFR|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS application form maintenance table will be used to store the application forms that are defined for every OCAS year.
These application forms are the ones to which the applicants would be applying for Admission (using the OCAS Web Application module)
at the institution.
SVROAFS|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS application form - section maintenance table will be used to store the configuration of the application forms and
the sections attached to the application form. A record will exist in this table for every section that is attached to a given application
form in an OCAS year.
SVROALC|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: OCAS Alert Code Rule Table
SVROALH|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: OCAS Alternate Program Header Table
SVROALP|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: OCAS Alternate Program Table
SVROANS|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS web user definable answer maintenance table will be used to store the configuration of the answers for a user defined question
marked as answer value type "H" (hard-coded) on SVROQUE (SVROQUE_QU_ANS_VAL_TYPE = H). Other characteristics of this table:
- This configuration is per question and year. - A record will exist in this table for every possible hard-coded answer to a given
question of hard-coded type defined in SVROQUE table. - The question for which the answers are being defined in this table would be
assigned to sections presented to the applicant in the application form when applying for Admission via the OCAS web application.
- All the records here are user definable.
SVROANT|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS web user definable answer table values maintenance table will be used to store the configuration of the answers for a
user defined question marked as answer value type "T" (list of values from a table) on SVROQUE (SVROQUE_QU_ANS_VAL_TYPE = T). Other characteristics
of this table: - This configuration is per question and year. - The configurations in this table are linked to questions that would be associated to
the web sections that would be attached to the OCAS web application form in a given year. - A record in this table represents the meta-data of a
question that will be used to construct the dynamic query (select statement) that when executed will retrieve the values that will identify the code
and description of the possible answers to the corresponding question (question defined in SVROQUE). These values would be all the possible
answers to the question (answer type T) that would be part of the application form presented to the applicant when applying for admission
via the OCAS web application module. - All the records here are user definable.

SVROFAS|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS web final additional services table will be used to store the web final additional services related data
that was originated in the OCAS web application. A record exists in this table for every time the applicant applies in a year (one record per OCAS year).
 This record represents the additional services information for the applicant in the OCAS year. The data in this table could come from the raw web
temporary additional services table (SVROWAS) or from direct updates applied by the user to the records.
SVROFAT|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS web final agent table will be used to store the web final agent data that was originated in the OCAS web application.
A record exists in this table for every time the applicant applies in a year (one record per OCAS year). This record represents the agent information
for the applicant in the OCAS year. The data in this table could come from the raw web temporary agent table (SVROWAT) or from direct updates applied
by the user to the records.
SVROFCC|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS web final contact in Canada table will be used to store the web final contact in Canada data that was originated in the OCAS web application.
A record exists in this table for every time the applicant applies in a year (one record per OCAS year).
This record represents the contact in Canada information for the applicant in the OCAS year. The data in this table could come from the raw web temporary agent table (SVROWCC) or from direct updates applied by the user to the records.
SVROFDQ|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS web final applicant response user definable questions table will be used to store the web final answers to user definable questions
that were originated in the OCAS web application. A record exists in this table for every answer to a user definable question that the applicant
has responded when applying in the OCAS year. Note that the answers to the pre-defined questions are stored in every specific table that has been
pre-defined for that matter (mailing address, e-mail, etc.). The data in this table could come from the raw web temporary applicant response user
definable table (SVROWDQ) or from direct updates applied by the user to the records. When the answer type is C (set of courses or tests),
then no record exists in this table for that type of question since the final answers for that case would be stored in SVROCGC for courses
(when SVROACT_ELEMENT_TYPE_IND is "C") and SVROCTC for tests (when SVROACT_ELEMENT_TYPE_IND is "T").
SVROFED|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS web final summary education table will be used to store the web final education data that was originated in the OCAS web application.
A record exists in this table for every time the applicant applies in a year (one record per OCAS year). The data in this table could come from
the raw web temporary education table (SVROWED) or from direct updates applied by the user to the records. This table holds a record for every
applicant in a given year that summarizes the final version of the educational background that the person has; however, it does not contain the
specifics of every study applicant may have done. For that, the SVROCEC table is used instead.
SVROFEM|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS web final employment table will be used to store the final employment information that was originated in the OCAS web application.
A record exists in this table for every time the applicant applies in a year (one record per OCAS year). The data in this table could come
from the raw web temporary employment table (SVROWEM) or from direct updates applied by the user to the records. Similar validations as the
ones associated to the address, phone and e-mail address in the AC records would be applied to the records in this table. A record exists
in this table for every time the applicant applies in a year (one record per OCAS year). This record represents the information of the most
recent company where the applicant is currently being employed.
SVROFHO|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS web final housing table will be used to store the web final housing data that was originated in the OCAS web application.
A record exists in this table for every time the applicant applies in a year (one record per OCAS year). This record represents the housing
information for the applicant in the OCAS year. The data in this table could come from the raw web temporary housing table (SVROWHO) or from
direct updates applied by the user to the records.
SVROFIT|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: OCAS Offer Data Files Tracking Table
SVROFLA|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS web final language table will be used to store the web final language data that was originated in the OCAS web application.
A record exists in this table for every time the applicant applies in a year (one record per OCAS year).
The data in this table could come from the raw web temporary language table (SVROWLA) or from direct updates applied by the user to the records.
SVROFSQ|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS application form - section - question maintenance table will be used to store the configuration of the application forms,
the sections attached to the application form and the specific configuration of the questions associated to the section in regards
to the application form to which the section is being attached to.
-  A record will exist in this table for every question associated to a section that is attached to a given application form in an OCAS year.
 -    The question in this record will inherit the configuration that the question had in the web section -
question maintenance table (SVROSEQ); however, in some cases that configuration can be overridden and stored in the
record of this table (SVROFSQ). - This will allow users to take a generic configuration of a section (from SVROSEQ)
and customize it for a specific application form (in SVROFSQ) in most of the cases (as long as the question is not marked as required in SVROSEQ).
SVROFTY|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS application form - applicant type maintenance table will be used to store the relationships between
the application forms and the applicant types for which they are valid in a given OCAS year. These application
forms are the ones to which applicants would be applying for admission.
SVROGEQ|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: OCAS Grade Equivalent Numeric Conversion Maintenance Table
SVROGTM|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS eligibility/scoring group code temporary table will be used to store temporary values
for OCAS Groups that are needed to select the Student Courses in Eligibility, Scoring and Alternate processing.
Due to the nature of the dynamic selection of courses, the required OCAS eligibility/scoring group codes need to
be stored in a temporary table so they are used in the couse/test selection.

SVROQUE|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS web user definable question maintenance table will be used to store the questions defined
by the users per year, that will be part of the sections presented to the applicant when applying for admission
via the OCAS web application.These user definable questions can be associated to the web sections that are attached
to the application form. Examples of user definable questions are: "why are you applying to this institution",
"do you plan to study post-grad studies in the future", etc. Note that these questions are different from the
pre-defined ones which are stored in SVVOPRQ instead.

SVROSEQ|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS web section - question maintenance table will be used to store the configuration
of the web sections and the questions associated to them in a given OCAS year. This configuration is independent
of the application form to which the section would be attached later on. These questions can fall in the
following categories: - Pre-defined questions (coming from SVROSPQ table); - User definable questions
(coming from SVROQUE table). Note that the type of section (defined in SVVOSTN) will be the one to determine
the types of questions that can be associated to the section. - In other words, if the section type is
pre-defined (SVVOSTN_SEC_TYPE = P), then the section  will allow ONLY pre-defined questions (the ones pre-defined
as system required seed data in SVROSPQ). - In other words, if the section type is user-definable (SVVOSTN_SEC_TYPE = U),
then the section will allow ONLY user definable questions (the ones set up in SVROQUE). Other characteristics of this table
are: Users will be allowed to adjust some of the fields associated to the delivered seed data such as: - Question answer
required system indicator (with some exceptions); - Sequence number; - Display indicator (with some exceptions); - Etc.
SVROSNU|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: OCAS Detail Course/Test Not Used by Program Scoring Table
SVROSPQ|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS web pre-defined section maintenance table will be used to store the configuration
of the pre-defined sections and the pre-defined questions.
SVROSTN|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: OCAS Stanine Numeric Conversion Maintenance Table
SVROSUS|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: OCAS Detail Course/Test Used by Program Scoring Table
SVROSVS|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: OCAS Offer Status VS Offer State Rule Table

SVROWAD|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS web temporary applicant data table will be used to store the raw web temporary applicant data (AC)
entered by the applicant via OCAS web application. This data is similar to the one in the SVRORAC table
therefore, the fields in SVROWAD will have similar characteristics/behavior as the ones in SVRORAC. When
applicable, it will use the same validations here as the ones already used in SVRORAC table. In addition other
fields related to the applicant are part of this table. - A record exists in this table for every OCAS applicant
that applied in a given OCAS year. - In general only one OCAS applicant number is associated to an applicant
in one year however, this table is prepared to allow multiple ones if future needs required to support that.
SVROWAS|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS web temporary additional services table will be used to store the raw web temporary additional services related data entered by the
 applicant via OCAS web application. A record exists in this table for every time the applicant applies in a year (one record per OCAS year). This record
 represents the additional services data for the applicant in the OCAS year.
SVROWAT|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS web temporary agent table will be used to store the raw web temporary agent related data entered
by the applicant via OCAS web application. A record exists in this table for every time the applicant applies in a year
(one record per OCAS year). This record represents the agent information for the applicant in the OCAS year.
SVROWCC|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS web temporary contact in Canada table will be used to store the raw web temporary
contact in Canada related data entered by the applicant via OCAS web application.A record exists
in this table for every time the applicant applies in a year (one record per OCAS year). This record
represents the contact in Canada information for the applicant in the OCAS year.
SVROWCR|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS web temporary course table will be used to store the raw web temporary course data (GC)
entered by the applicant via OCAS web application. This data is similar to the one in the SVRORGC table
therefore, the fields in SVROWCR will have similar characteristics/behavior as the ones in SVRORGC.
When applicable, it will use the same validations here as the ones already used in SVRORGC table.
A record exists in this table for every course that the applicant has declared has taken or is currently taking.
SVROWDQ|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS web temporary applicant response user definable questions table will be used to
store the raw web temporary answers to user definable questions entered by the applicant via
OCAS web application. A record exists in this table for every answer to a user definable question
that the applicant has responded when applying in the OCAS year. Note that the answers to the pre-defined
questions are stored in every specific table that has been pre-defined for that matter (mailing address, e-mail, etc.).
When the answer type is C (set of courses or tests), then no record exists in this table for that type of question since
the temporary answers for that case would be stored in SVROWCR for courses (when SVROACT_ELEMENT_TYPE_IND is "C")
and SVROWTS for tests (when SVROACT_ELEMENT_TYPE_IND is "T").
SVROWEC|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS web temporary detail education table will be used to store the raw web temporary detail
education data entered by the applicant via OCAS web application. This table holds a record for every detail
of educational background that applicants provides when filling an application for a given year. A record exists
in this table for every combination of institution, program, etc. that applicant may have declared as studied or
currently studying. In order to save a record in this table, there should be a value for the EDUCATIONAL INSTITUTE
CODE (SVROWEC_EDUC_OBSI_CODE) or for the EDUCATIONAL INSTITUTE NAME (SVROWEC_EDUC_INST_NAME) at least. Similar
validations should be applied as the one applied to the raw data stored in SVROREC table.
SVROWED|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS web temporary summary education table will be used to store the raw web temporary education data
entered by the applicant via OCAS web application. This table holds a record for every applicant in a given year
that summarizes the educational background that the person has mostly related to Ontario (OCAS clients); however,
it does not contain the specifics of every study applicant may have done. For that, the SVROWEC table
(similar to SVROREC) is used instead. Although this data is pre-defined, users that are outside Ontario are not
obligated to use it since as indicated this is very particular to Ontario. A record exists in this table for
every time the applicant applies in a year (one record per OCAS year).
SVROWEM|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS web temporary employment table will be used to store the raw web temporary employment information entered by
the applicant via OCAS web application. Similar validations as the ones associated to the address, phone and e-mail address
in the AC records would be applied to the records in this table. A record exists in this table for every time the applicant
applies in a year (one record per OCAS year). This record represents the information of the most recent company where the
applicant is currently being employed.
SVROWHO|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS web temporary housing table will be used to store the raw web temporary housing related data entered by the applicant
via OCAS web application. A record exists in this table for every time the applicant applies in a year (one record per OCAS year).
This record represents the housing information for the applicant in the OCAS year. A record should exist in this table whenever
SVROWAS_HM_STAY_SERV_IND is set to (yes) Y.
SVROWLA|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS web temporary language table will be used to store the raw web temporary language data
entered by the applicant via OCAS web application. A record exists in this table for every time the applicant
applies in a year (one record per OCAS year).
SVROWLQ|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: OCAS Waitlist Queue Table
SVROWPC|TABLE|CANDA OCAS: The OCAS web temporary program choice table will be used to store the raw web temporary program choice (CC)

the fields in SVROWPC will have similar characteristics/behavior as the ones in SVRORCC. When applicable, it will use
the same validations here as the ones already used in SVRORCC table. A record exists in this table for every program
that the applicant has chosen to apply in the OCAS year, term and semester.
SVROWSQ|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS web applicant security question - answer table will be used to store the questions and answers that the applicant number will be using to recover his/her PIN when required.
SVROWTS|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS web temporary test table will be used to store the raw web temporary test data (TC) entered by the

SVVOPRQ|TABLE|CANADA OCAS: The OCAS web pre-defined question validation table will be used to store the codes that will identify the pre-defined questions
that will be associated to web pre-defined sections that will be attached to an OCAS application form.
Examples of pre-defined questions are: Title, Last name, first name, gender, birth date, social insurance number (SIN), second name,
previous last name, e-mail, etc. - These questions will be assigned to sections that will be mandatory through all the applications
and OCAS years. - They are usually mandatory and the answer to them provided by the applicants when filling the OCAS application
form will be stored in specific pre-defined places (for both: temporary and final OCAS data). - They are defined once,
that is why OCAS year is not present.

WCHFCON|TABLE|Contract History Table (updated for every change to WCBFCON) For comments, see the appropriate column comment on WCBFCON
WCHFDSP|TABLE|Dispositional History Table. This table lists all the dispositions that a contract has been at (including currently), as well as the reasons for th emove, and who moved it.
WCQFCON|TABLE|Contract Event Queue table. This table contains events generated by other actions in the system - like changing the instructor assigned to the section.
WCRCACC|TABLE|Contract Accounting Table.
WCRDERR|TABLE|Dispositional Error Table.
WCRFCTL|TABLE|Control Settings for the Contract System
WCRLOGS|TABLE|Activity Logs
WCRMEET|TABLE|Meeting Times Table. Filled in only if the contract has no CRN, OR, if the meeting times for the contract need to be different than the section times
WCRPAYR|TABLE|Pay Rule Table. Determines pay and other factors based on a series of criteria specified in WCRRPYR (essentially, if the rules in WCRRPYR are met, then the values in this table are supplied to the contract being created)
WCRPOSR|TABLE|Position Rule Table. This table maps contracts generated in a given department with given contract types to a position code in HR. Use only for highly generic rules, i.e., all online classes get OL9000 position code; specific positions that are based on the type of pay can be defined on the pay rule table. Highly usable for the case where different departments get different positions, even though they may have the same type of pay.
WCRRPYR|TABLE|Repeating table for WCRPAYR; specifies the actual criteria for rules
WCRUSRS|TABLE|User Security Table. This table defines who can access the contract system and what rights they can have. The user must also exist in GOBEACC. This table is technically repeating; if a user appears more than once they will have access to all the specified departments (with the rights incurred by each instance). However the user must specify their department before using the form to edit contracts (otherwise the system picks the first rule it finds - which may not match up to the user's expectations).
WCTCPRL|TABLE|Temporary table used during automatic contract generation.

WCVDISP|TABLE|Disposition Validation Table. This table is the master list for all the possible states a contract can be in. Must have a 00 entry (this is where all contracts start).
